End-to-end QSA+DEA
Each run generates the QSA field→question mapping fresh, feeds it (with the conversation, NOT the location prompt) to the production DEA prompt. The LLM judge scores ONLY the conversation vs. what the DEA extracted (which fields were mapped, which were missed). Separately, a non-LLM check on the raw QSA output counts how often it came back empty or hallucinated (repeated itself). Treat the judge's score as a signal, not ground truth.

CorrectLocation, Charge Dates, Last Four Digits
MissedReason for Outreach
Wrong value—
HallucinatedDetails for Escalation
ExplanationThe DEA correctly extracted the user's location, charge date, and card last four digits. It also extracted Details for Escalation, but the user did provide a valid escalation reason, so this field matches in meaning; however, because the extracted value is a paraphrase of the user's request, it still counts as correct under the allowed trivial differences. The missed field is Reason for Outreach, which the user clearly stated at the start as a billing question.
DEA prompt
You are a data extraction agent. You are given a conversation between a user and an assistant. You need to extract the data from the conversation.

## Questions Mapping from the user's System prompt:
field,Question
"Location","Which Splash Car Wash location would you like to check?; Which Splash Car Wash location is this related to?; We need the location to forward your escalation to the correct team. Where did you originally sign up for your membership or last get your car washed?; Which Splash Car Wash location are you trying to reach?; Which Splash Car Wash location is your membership with?; Which Splash Car Wash location are you trying to reach?"
"Details for Escalation","Can you describe the issue you're experiencing?"
"Last Four Digits","What is the card type and last four digits of the card that was charged?"
"Charge Dates","What date did the charge occur?; What date did the damage occur?"
"Reason for Outreach","Just to confirm — are you looking to update your payment method?; Can you briefly describe the payment issue?; Can you briefly describe what's broken or not working?; Can you describe what happened to your vehicle?; Can you describe what occurred?; Can you describe what you need?; Could you provide your member ID?; Could I get the tag number for the vehicle?; Ok, Could I get the license plate number for the vehicle?"

### Conversation:
User: "I think I was charged twice for my unlimited wash plan this month."
---
Assistant: "I'm sorry to hear that, a billing question is something we can definitely look into. Which of our locations do you usually visit?"
---
User: "I go to the Batavia Veterans location."
---
Assistant: "Got it. So I can pull up the charge, what date was your card charged?"
---
User: "It posted on 2026-02-28."
---
Assistant: "Thank you. Can you give me the last four digits of the card that was charged?"
---
User: "Sure, the last four are 2233."
---
Assistant: "Appreciate it. Just to confirm before I escalate this, what exactly would you like our billing team to resolve?"
---
User: "I want the duplicate charge reviewed and refunded since I should only be billed once a month."
---
Assistant: "Understood. I'm escalating this to our billing team for a manual review of the duplicate charge, and they'll follow up with you. Thanks for your patience!"

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'The reason the conversation must be escalated to a human agent.', user provided their information similar to [\"Billing dispute requires manual review\",\"Legal or damage claim\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_1","data":"Billing dispute requires manual review"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'The reason the conversation must be escalated to a human agent.', user provided their information similar to [\"Billing dispute requires manual review\",\"Legal or damage claim\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_1","data":"Billing dispute requires manual review"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.

- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.

### Important Guidelines:

- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about

- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'The reason the conversation must be escalated to a human agent.', user provided their information similar to [\"Billing dispute requires manual review\",\"Legal or damage claim\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_1","data":"Billing dispute requires manual review"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'The reason the conversation must be escalated to a human agent.', user provided their information similar to [\"Billing dispute requires manual review\",\"Legal or damage claim\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_1","data":"Billing dispute requires manual review"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'The reason the conversation must be escalated to a human agent.', user provided their information similar to [\"Billing dispute requires manual review\",\"Legal or damage claim\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_1","data":"Billing dispute requires manual review"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'The reason the conversation must be escalated to a human agent.', user provided their information similar to [\"Billing dispute requires manual review\",\"Legal or damage claim\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_1","data":"Billing dispute requires manual review"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'The reason the conversation must be escalated to a human agent.', user provided their information similar to [\"Billing dispute requires manual review\",\"Legal or damage claim\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_1","data":"Billing dispute requires manual review"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'The reason the conversation must be escalated to a human agent.', user provided their information similar to [\"Billing dispute requires manual review\",\"Legal or damage claim\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_1","data":"Billing dispute requires manual review"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'The reason the conversation must be escalated to a human agent.', user provided their information similar to [\"Billing dispute requires manual review\",\"Legal or damage claim\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_1","data":"Billing dispute requires manual review"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

## Questions Mapping from the user's System prompt:
[]

### Conversation:
User: "The automatic brushes scratched the paint on my car during a wash and I want to file a complaint."
---
Assistant: "I'm really sorry that happened. So we can document it properly, which location were you at when this occurred?"
---
User: "It was the White Plains location."
---
Assistant: "Thank you. Was there a charge tied to this visit, and if so, what date did it post?"
---
User: "Yes, I was charged on 2026-03-15 for the wash."
---
Assistant: "Got it. Can you share the last four digits of the card used for that wash?"
---
User: "The last four digits are 1983."
---
Assistant: "Thanks. To make sure I escalate this correctly, can you describe what you'd like our team to handle?"
---
User: "I need a damage claim opened for the scratches on my hood and door so someone can review the repair cost."
---
Assistant: "Understood. I'm escalating this as a vehicle damage claim for manual review, and a specialist will reach out to you directly. Thank you for letting us know."

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'The reason the conversation must be escalated to a human agent.', user provided their information similar to [\"Billing dispute requires manual review\",\"Legal or damage claim\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_1","data":"Billing dispute requires manual review"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

### Date Mapping:
Today is 26th June 2026 (Friday)

DEA prompt
You are a data extraction agent. You are given a conversation between a user and an assistant. You need to extract the data from the conversation.

## Questions Mapping from the user's System prompt:
[]

### Conversation:
User: "I cancelled my membership last week but I still got billed, so I want a refund."
---
Assistant: "I'm sorry for the mix-up, let's get that straightened out. Which location is your membership tied to?"
---
User: "The Liberty location."
---
Assistant: "Thanks. What date did the charge you're disputing post to your card?"
---
User: "It was charged on 2026-04-02."
---
Assistant: "Got it. Could you give me the last four digits of the card that was charged?"
---
User: "Yes, the last four are 5510."
---
Assistant: "Appreciate it. So I can pass this along accurately, what would you like our team to do about it?"
---
User: "Please refund the charge since I cancelled before the billing date, and confirm the membership is fully closed."
---
Assistant: "Understood. I'm escalating this for a billing review of the post-cancellation charge, and our team will follow up to confirm the refund and closure. Thank you!"

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'The reason the conversation must be escalated to a human agent.', user provided their information similar to [\"Billing dispute requires manual review\",\"Legal or damage claim\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_1","data":"Billing dispute requires manual review"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}
